
##### Early Debug Events #####

country_event = {
    id = 777770400
    title = "Debug Event to set ai Victors"
    desc = "Random nations will be considered a secondary victors."
    fire_only_once = yes
    is_triggered_only = yes
    option = {
        name = "Huzzah!"
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				ai = yes
				OR = { has_global_flag = Total_Two_Victor has_global_flag = Total_Three_Victor has_global_flag = Total_Four_Victor has_global_flag = Total_Five_Victor has_global_flag = Total_Six_Victor has_global_flag = Total_Seven_Victor has_global_flag = Total_Eight_Victor }
			}
			set_variable = { which = Second_Victor value = 1 }
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				ai = yes
				OR = { has_global_flag = Total_Three_Victor has_global_flag = Total_Four_Victor has_global_flag = Total_Five_Victor has_global_flag = Total_Six_Victor has_global_flag = Total_Seven_Victor has_global_flag = Total_Eight_Victor }
			}
			set_variable = { which = Third_Victor value = 1 }
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				ai = yes
				OR = { has_global_flag = Total_Four_Victor has_global_flag = Total_Five_Victor has_global_flag = Total_Six_Victor has_global_flag = Total_Seven_Victor has_global_flag = Total_Eight_Victor }
			}
			set_variable = { which = Fourth_Victor value = 1 }
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				ai = yes
				OR = { has_global_flag = Total_Five_Victor has_global_flag = Total_Six_Victor has_global_flag = Total_Seven_Victor has_global_flag = Total_Eight_Victor }
			}
			set_variable = { which = Fifth_Victor value = 1 }
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				ai = yes
				OR = { has_global_flag = Total_Six_Victor has_global_flag = Total_Seven_Victor has_global_flag = Total_Eight_Victor }
			}
			set_variable = { which = Sixth_Victor value = 1 }
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				ai = yes
				OR = { has_global_flag = Total_Seven_Victor has_global_flag = Total_Eight_Victor }
			}
			set_variable = { which = Seventh_Victor value = 1 }
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				ai = yes
				has_global_flag = Total_Eight_Victor
			}
			set_variable = { which = Eighth_Victor value = 1 }
		}
    }
}

country_event = {
    id = 777770401
    title = "Self Tag War Debug Major"
    desc = "This nation will be considered a major vanquished state."
    fire_only_once = yes
    is_triggered_only = yes
    option = {
        name = "Huzzah!"
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				is_greater_power = yes
				ai = yes
			}
			set_variable = { which = Major_Defeated value = 1 }
		}
    }
}

##### Initalizing Conference #####

country_event = {
    id = 777770403
    title = "The $CAPITAL$ Conference has been called!"
    desc = "This decision is to inform you the following events will allow you to dismantle recent enemies."
	major = yes
    is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		#sets defeated value for newly defeated countries
		set_global_flag = waiting_for_victor_update
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				exists = yes
				has_country_flag = Major_Defeated
			}
			clr_country_flag = Major_Defeated
			random_owned = {
				limit = { owner = { check_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 0.99 } NOT = { check_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 1.99 } } } }
				owner = { set_variable = { which = Major_Defeated value = 1 } set_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 0 } }
			}
			random_owned = {
				limit = { owner = { check_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 1.99 } NOT = { check_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 2.99 } } } }
				owner = { set_variable = { which = Major_Defeated value = 2 } set_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 0 } }
			}
			random_owned = {
				limit = { owner = { check_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 2.99 } NOT = { check_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 3.99 } } } }
				owner = { set_variable = { which = Major_Defeated value = 3 } set_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 0 } }
			}
			random_owned = {
				limit = { owner = { check_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 3.99 } NOT = { check_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 4.99 } } } }
				owner = { set_variable = { which = Major_Defeated value = 4 } set_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 0 } }
			}
			random_owned = {
				limit = { owner = { check_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 4.99 } NOT = { check_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 5.99 } } } }
				owner = { set_variable = { which = Major_Defeated value = 5 } set_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 0 } }
			}
			random_owned = {
				limit = { owner = { check_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 5.99 } NOT = { check_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 6.99 } } } }
				owner = { set_variable = { which = Major_Defeated value = 6 } set_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 0 } }
			}
			random_owned = {
				limit = { owner = { check_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 6.99 } NOT = { check_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 7.99 } } } }
				owner = { set_variable = { which = Major_Defeated value = 7 } set_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 0 } }
			}
			random_owned = {
				limit = { owner = { check_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 7.99 } NOT = { check_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 8.99 } } } }
				owner = { set_variable = { which = Major_Defeated value = 8 } set_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 0 } }
			}
		}
	}
	
    option = {
        name = "Very Well"
		clr_global_flag = waiting_for_victor_update
		
		#sets conference value for current country
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					check_variable = { which = dismantlement_leader value = 0.99 }
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = dismantlement_leader value = 1.99 } }
					NOT = { war_countries = { check_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 0.99 } NOT = { check_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 1.99 } } } }
				}
			}
			owner = {
				set_variable = { which = conference value = 1 }
				set_variable = { which = dismantlement_leader value = 0 }
				set_global_flag = Dismantlement_Underway_1
				set_variable = { which = Dismantlement_Chair value = 1 }
			}
		}
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					check_variable = { which = dismantlement_leader value = 1.99 }
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = dismantlement_leader value = 2.99 } }
					NOT = { war_countries = { check_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 1.99 } NOT = { check_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 2.99 } } } }
				}
			}
			owner = {
				set_variable = { which = conference value = 2 }
				set_variable = { which = dismantlement_leader value = 0 }
				set_global_flag = Dismantlement_Underway_2
				set_variable = { which = Dismantlement_Chair value = 2 }
			}
		}
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					check_variable = { which = dismantlement_leader value = 2.99 }
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = dismantlement_leader value = 3.99 } }
					NOT = { war_countries = { check_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 2.99 } NOT = { check_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 3.99 } } } }
				}
			}
			owner = {
				set_variable = { which = conference value = 3 }
				set_variable = { which = dismantlement_leader value = 0 }
				set_global_flag = Dismantlement_Underway_3
				set_variable = { which = Dismantlement_Chair value = 3 }
			}
		}
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					check_variable = { which = dismantlement_leader value = 3.99 }
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = dismantlement_leader value = 4.99 } }
					NOT = { war_countries = { check_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 3.99 } NOT = { check_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 4.99 } } } }

			}
			owner = {

				set_variable = { which = dismantlement_leader value = 0 }
				set_global_flag = Dismantlement_Underway_4
				set_variable = { which = Dismantlement_Chair value = 4 }

			}

				set_variable = { which = dismantlement_leader value = 0 }
				set_global_flag = Dismantlement_Underway_5
				set_variable = { which = Dismantlement_Chair value = 5 }
			}
		}
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					check_variable = { which = dismantlement_leader value = 5.99 }
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = dismantlement_leader value = 6.99 } }

			}
			owner = {
				set_variable = { which = conference value = 6 }
				set_variable = { which = dismantlement_leader value = 0 }
				set_global_flag = Dismantlement_Underway_6
				set_variable = { which = Dismantlement_Chair value = 6 }

				owner = {
					check_variable = { which = dismantlement_leader value = 6.99 }
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = dismantlement_leader value = 7.99 } }

				set_global_flag = Dismantlement_Underway_7

		random_owned = {

					NOT = { check_variable = { which = part_of_conference value = 1.99 } }
					NOT = { war_countries = { check_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 0.99 } NOT = { check_variable = { which = target_of_dismantlement value = 1.99 } } } }

				set_global_flag = Dismantlement_Underway_1
				set_variable = { which = Dismantlement_Chair value = 1 }

country_event = {
    id = 777770406
    title = "How we are to be treated in defeat must now be considered"
    desc = "We will now be dismantled."
	allow_multiple_instances = yes
    is_triggered_only = yes
    option = {
        name = "Very Well"
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				any_core = {
					owner = {
						check_variable = { which = Major_Defeated value = 0.99 }
					}
				}
				exists = yes
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = Freedom_Event_Sent value = 0.99 } }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = Major_Defeated value = 0.99 } }
			}
			country_event = 777770409
			set_variable = { which = Outcome_Required value = 1 }
			set_variable = { which = Freedom_Event_Sent value = 1 }
			set_variable = { which = Rewritable_State value = 0 }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				any_core = {
					owner = {
						check_variable = { which = Major_Defeated value = 0.99 }
					}
				}
				exists = no
				NOT = { tag = UBD }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = Freedom_Event_Sent value = 0.99 } }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = Major_Defeated value = 0.99 } }
			}
			country_event = 777770408
			set_variable = { which = Outcome_Required value = 1 }
			set_variable = { which = Freedom_Event_Sent value = 1 }
			set_variable = { which = Rewritable_State value = 1 }
		}
		any_country = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = Dismantlement_Chair value = 0.99 }
				exists = yes
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = Major_Defeated value = 0.99 } }
				OR = {
					1729 = { owner = { tag = THIS } }
					1730 = { owner = { tag = THIS } }
				}
			}
			country_event = 777770600
		}
		CLN = { country_event = 4778747 }
    }
}

    option = {
        name = "$FROMCOUNTRY$ shall cores from remaining lands"
		FROM = {
			set_variable = { which = Existing_NonOverwrite value = 1 }
			country_event = 777770460
		}
		create_alliance = FROM
    }
    option = {
        name = "We do not care about $FROMCOUNTRY$"
		FROM = {
			set_variable = { which = Existing_Apathy value = 1 }
			country_event = 777770460
		}
    }
    option = {
        name = "$FROMCOUNTRY$ shall not grow larger"
		FROM = {
			set_variable = { which = Existing_As_Is value = 1 }
			country_event = 777770460
		}
    }
    option = {
        name = "The lands of $FROMCOUNTRY$ shall be ours"
		FROM = {
			set_variable = { which = Existing_Chomp value = 1 }
			country_event = 777770460	
		}
    }

##### Colonial Events #####

country_event = {
    id = 777770600
    title = "$FROMCOUNTRY_ADJ$ Tunisia!"
    desc = "$FROMCOUNTRY$ currently has holdings in Tunisia, What should be done with them?"
    is_triggered_only = yes
    option = {
        name = "We shall take them for ourselves."
        any_country = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { check_variable = { which = Major_Defeated value = 0.99 } }
				check_variable = { which = Major_Defeated value = 0.99 }
				tag = FROM
			}
            set_country_flag = Lost_Tunisia
        }
    }
    option = {
        name = "We do not care about Tunisia."
    }
    option = {
        name = "They shall remain with the defeated."
    }
}

country_event = {
    id = 777770700
    title = "The Tunisia Plan!"
    desc = "Tunisia shall be given to a victorious power"
    is_triggered_only = yes
    option = {
        name = "We shall take them for ourselves."
        random_country = {
			limit = {
				ai = yes
			}
            any_owned = { limit = { OR = { province_id = 1730 province_id = 1729 } } secede_province = THIS }
        }
    }
}
